<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">само-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наде́ять(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadéjatʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-янный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самонадеянный.html>самонаде́янный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">samonadéjannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>arrogant, presumptuous, assuming, assumptive</li>
<li>overweening <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">over-confident</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>self-confident, confident, self-assured, self-sufficient</li>
<li>presuming</li>
<li>reliant</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">само-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:самоуважение.html>самоуваже́ние</a> (30402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:самоучка.html>самоу́чка</a> (24290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">само-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самоучка.html>самоу́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">samoúčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самоучка.html>самоу́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самоучка.html>самоу́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самоучка.html>самоу́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>self-taught, autodidact, automath</li></ol>

***самый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> (58)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sámyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">definitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the very, the selfsame, the very same
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:центр.html>це́нтре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́рода</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мого</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рка</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja živú v <b>sámom</b> céntre góroda u <b>sámovo</b> párka.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I live in <b>the very</b> center of town close to the park.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>и́менно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мое</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná dúmala ímenno tó že <b>sámoje</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She thinks exactly <b>the same</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>the most <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">superlative degree</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">санкт-петербу́рг <b><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красивый.html>краси́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> росси́и.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sankt-Peterbúrg <b>sámyj</b> krasívyj górod v Rossíi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Saint Petersburg is <b>the most</b> beautiful city in Russia.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Скафти <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поколотить.html>поколоти́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́та</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> Стема <a href = vnd.unilang:вмешаться.html>вмеша́лся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:разнять.html>разня́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поработать.html>порабо́тает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>весло́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого</a></b> росто́ва.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skafti jedvá ne pokolotíl bráta, no Stema vmešálsja, raznjál, skazáv, što porabótajet veslóm do <b>samovo</b> Rostóva.</i></dd><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
